add_namespace = plx

### Introduction
country_event = {
	id = plx.1
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.1" }
	title = plx.1.t
	desc = plx.1.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plx.1.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom
			
			#end_coalition = yes
			
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes	
			add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
		}
		country_event = {
			id = plxv2.018 days = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	#option = {
	#	name = plx.1.b
	#
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		factor = 0
	#	}
	#
	#}
}

### Black Monday Hits Poland
country_event = {
	id = plx.2
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.2" }
	title = plx.2.t
	desc = plx.2.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plx.2.a
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = -0.50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		#remove_ideas = PLX_PL_rapid_growth
		#add_ideas = PLX_PL_econ_depression_4
		#add_ideas = PLX_PL_econ_depression_fiscal_4
		#add_ideas = PLX_PL_econ_depression_social_4
		
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_political_power_gain = 0.10
			tooltip = political_power_gain_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = -0.20 
			tooltip = production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = -0.40
			tooltip = production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_industrial_capacity_factory = -0.15
			tooltip = industrial_capacity_factory_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.50
			tooltip = production_speed_buildings_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_research_speed_factor = -0.15
			tooltip = research_speed_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_consumer_goods_factor = -0.10
			tooltip = consumer_goods_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_line_change_production_efficiency_factor = -0.10 
			tooltip = line_change_production_efficiency_factor_tt
		}	
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_supply_factor = -0.10
			tooltip = supply_consumption_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_local_resources_factor = -0.10 
			tooltip = local_resources_factor_tt
		}
		add_to_variable = { 
			PLX_indutry_conscription_factor = 0.30 
			tooltip = conscription_factor_tt
		}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = PLX_germany_weaker_control_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = PLX_PL_econ_collapse
			end_puppet = GER
			#country_event = {
			#	id = plx.23 days = 320
			#} 
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	#option = {
	#	name = plx.2.b
	#
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		factor = 0
	#	}
	#
	#}
}

#Army Coup
country_event = {
	id = plx.4
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.4" }
	title = plx.4.t
	desc = plx.4.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plx.4.a
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.10
		remove_ideas = PLX_PL_army_within_state
		#add_ideas = PLX_coup_aftermath_2		
		custom_effect_tooltip = PLX_military_coup_tooltip		
		hidden_effect = {
		
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Walery Sławek "
				picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Walery_Slawek_kx.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = red_tinted_autocracy_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = POL_zlp_party_long
				name = "ZLP"
			}
			
			
			country_event = {
				id = plx.38 days = 3
			}
			GER_remove_from_mitteleuropa = yes
			leave_faction = yes
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = POL_german_commander }
				set_nationality = GER
				remove_unit_leader_trait = POL_german_commander
			}
			remove_ideas = POL_warsaw_garrison
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = plxf.16 days = 7
				}
			}
			
			set_country_flag = plx_social_coup
			set_country_flag = plx_zlp_coup
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				POL_Welery_Slawek_hog_pau
				POL_Boleslaw_Wieniawa_Dlugoszewski_for_pau
				POL_Stanislaw_Szeptycki_eco_pau
				#POL_Eugeniusz_Kwiatkowski_eco_tot
				POL_Marian_Kukiel_sec_pau
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.15
			}	
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.05
			}	

			end_coalition = yes
			
			add_tot_to_coalition = yes
			
			
			country_event = {
				id = plx.10 days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = plx.26
				days = 7
			}			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	#option = {
	#	name = plx.4.b
	#
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		factor = 0
	#	}
	#
	#}
}

###Cut-off from Germany or Not
country_event = {
	id = plx.8
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.8" }
	title = plx.8.t
	desc = plx.8.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_ready_to_go_foreign }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plx.8.a	
		add_political_power = 50
		custom_effect_tooltip = PLX_leave_germany_tooltip	
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = plx.38 days = 3
			}
			GER_remove_from_mitteleuropa = yes
			leave_faction = yes
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = POL_german_commander }
				set_nationality = GER
				remove_unit_leader_trait = POL_german_commander
			}
			remove_ideas = POL_warsaw_garrison
			remove_ideas = PLX_PL_paying_for_garrison
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = plxf.16 days = 7
				} 
			}
			
			set_country_flag = POL_ready_to_go_foreign		
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}		
	}

	option = {
		name = plx.8.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_endecja_rules }
			#NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			#NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = POL_ready_to_go_foreign		
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
	}
}

###Army Cements Power
country_event = {
	id = plx.10
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.10" }
	title = plx.10.t
	desc = plx.10.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plx.10.a
		add_political_power = 20
		add_stability = 0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = PLX_legionists_alone_tooltip
		hidden_effect = { 
			#drop_cosmetic_tag = yes 
			set_cosmetic_tag = POL_orange_republic
			set_country_flag = plx_zlp_rules
			set_country_flag = POL_ready_to_go_foreign
			
			complete_national_focus = KX_PL_ZL_TAKES_POWER	

			country_event = {
				id = plx.32 days = 2
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = plxv2.124 days = 30
			}			
			country_event = {
				id = plxv2.072 days = 45
			}			
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = plx.10.b
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}

			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Józef Chaciński "
				#desc = "POLITICS_JOZEF_CHACINSKI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Jozef_Chacinski.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = christian_democracy_subtype
			}	
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Roman Rybarski "
				picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Roman_Rybarski.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = national_democracy_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {

			}

	}

		name = plx.39.a
		add_stability = -0.10

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_natal }
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_intermarium_natal
			}		
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_falanga_party }
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_intermarian_falanga_party
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = plx_falanga_wins }

				limit = { has_country_flag = plx_natdem_radical_young_victory }

				limit = {

						has_government = totalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_intermarian_council
			}

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_kingdom }

					OR = {

						has_country_leader = { name = "Augustyn I" ruling_only = yes }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Stanisław III" ruling_only = yes }

country_event = {
	id = plx.41 #Left-PPS Presidents
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.41" }
	title = plx.41.t
	desc = plx.41.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = plx.41.a #Barlicki
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_gomulka }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_dubois }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_tuwim }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_zulawski }
		}
		#increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_2 = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } } 
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Karol II Olbracht"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Karol_Olbracht.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype #ideology = radsoc_revisionist_marxism_subtype
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Norbert Barlicki "
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Norbert_Barlicki.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype #ideology = radsoc_revisionist_marxism_subtype
				}
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 60
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = POL_pps_soc_party
				name = "PPS"
			}			
			country_event = {
				id = plx.41 days = 1830
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				POL_Norbert_Barlicki_hog_sde
				POL_Eugenia_Pragierowa_for_rso
				POL_Michal_Kalecki_eco_rso #POL_Stanislaw_Niemyski_eco_rso
				POL_Ludwik_Cohn_sec_rso
			}			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = plx_lange_econ }
				remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
				add_ideas = POL_Oskar_Lange_eco_tot				
			}			
			end_coalition = yes
			add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = plx.41.b #Dubois
		trigger = { 
			#NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } } 
			has_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_dubois
		}
		#increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}		
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } } 
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Karol II Olbracht"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Karol_Olbracht.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Stanisław Dubois "
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_PLX_Stanislaw_Dubois.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
				}
			}
			
			meta_effect = {

country_event = {
	id = plx.42 #Elections in Socialist Poland
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plx.42" 
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_not_dem
		}
	}
	title = plx.42.t
	desc = plx.42.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = plx.42.a
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = PLX_elections_every_5y_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_cosmetic_tag = POL_intermarian 
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_intermarian_soc
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = POL_peoples_soc
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 60
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}	
			country_event = {
				id = plx.41 days = 1830
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_ppsd_exists }
				}
				add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
			}

			set_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_not_dem		
		}
	}
}

##Gomulka on top
country_event = {
	id = plxv2.053
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plxv2.053" }
	title = plxv2.053.t
	desc = plxv2.053.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = plx.53.a #Gomulka
		set_country_flag = plx_rad_pps_gomulka
		
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes } } 
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Karol II Olbracht"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Karol_Olbracht.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radsoc_communism_subtype
				}				
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Władysław Gomułka "
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_PLX_Wladyslaw_Gomulka.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radsoc_communism_subtype
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				POL_Wladyslaw_Gomulka_hog_rso
				POL_Antonina_Sokolicz_for_rso
				POL_Oskar_Lange_eco_tot
				POL_Edward_Bonislawski_sec_rso
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = plx_kalecki_econ }
				remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister
				add_ideas = POL_Michal_Kalecki_eco_rso				
			}			
			
			#meta_effect = {
			#	text = {
			#		set_politics = {
			#			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			#			last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
			#			election_frequency = 60
			#			elections_allowed = yes
			#		}
			#	}
			#	CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			#}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = POL_pps_soc_party
				name = "PPS"
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			#add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
			country_event = {
				id = plxv2.054
				days = 8
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = { 
			#		has_completed_focus = KX_PL_AS_BUTCHERS_OF_DEMOCRACY 
			#		NOT = { has_country_flag = plx_slawek_dead }
			#	}
			#	country_event = {
			#		id = plxv2.104
			#		days = 12
			#	}
			#}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = plxv2.105 #
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plxv2.105" }
	title = plxv2.105.t
	desc = plxv2.105.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = plxv2.105.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = plx_socdem_chadecja
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = POL_chnpp_party_long
				name = "ChNPP"
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { name = "Karol II Olbracht" ruling_only = yes }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Karol II Olbracht"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Karol_Olbracht.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_paternal_socialism_subtype
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Adam Chądzyński "
					picture = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Adam_Chadzynski.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_paternal_socialism_subtype
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			
			end_coalition = yes
			add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
			add_soccon_to_coalition = yes			
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 1
		}
	}

		name = plxv2.135.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}	
}

country_event = {
	id = plxv2.138
	#immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event plxv2.138" }
	title = plxv2.138.t
	desc = plxv2.138.d
	#picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = plxv2.138.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
				election_frequency = 120
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = KX_PL_PG_LIMIT_ROYAL_PREROGATIVES }
				set_country_leader_ideology = autdem_christian_democracy_subtype
			}
			else = {
				set_country_leader_ideology = prussian_constitutionalism_subtype
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				POL_Wladyslaw_Sikorski_hog_pau
				POL_Stanislaw_Stronski_for_sco
				POL_Adam_Chadzynski_eco_sco
				POL_Maciej_Rataj_sec_sli
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = POL_zjkp_party_long
				name = "ZJKP"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = POL_zjkp_party_long
				name = "ZJKP"
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
			add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
			add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
			
			country_event = {
				id = plxv2.140 days = 1835
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat

				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = KX_PL_PG_GOVERNMENT_BY_APPOINTMENT }
				set_country_leader_ideology = prussian_constitutionalism_subtype
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = KX_PL_PG_SEEK_LEGITIMACY_IN_PEOPLE }

				KRK_Henryk_Werynski_for_tot

				POL_Waclaw_Pyszkowski_sec_tot
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = 100
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
